This place is Amazing!! I've lived just down the street for years & only recently discovered it.
Delicious treats, refreshing agua fresca, sandwich croissants, & the made-to-order crepes are absolutely scrumptious.
They don't just make sweet crepes either, you can get something savoury for a great brunch there as well (e.g. the jalisco, ham & cheese, or even a quiche).<//review>

< review>
I‚Äôve been a regular customer for months now, and I can confidently say that Xielo Artisan Desserts is an excellent caf√©!  Not only is the menu varied with delicious options for all palates, but they use high quality ingredients, have wonderful presentation, and keep surprising you as you continue to visit!  The owner, Juan, humbly shares that his family who put together their recipies are the artists, and essentially he‚Äôs just the business side making it available to people.  Well their family has been in the food industry for many years tracing back to Mexico, and they have recipies that his grandmother made 60 years ago! My favorites are the Berry French Cream sweet crepe with extra BFC, the albondigas soup (best I‚Äôve ever had), and my custom cajeta & lechera, light ice, extra coffee frappe!  Five honorable mentions are the guayaba y queso empanadas, the cajeta con nuez sweet crepe with a scoop of ice cream on top, the monte alban sweet crepe, the requeson, and the cafe de olla (can you tell I have a sweet tooth? ü§£). The caf√© has a relaxing atmosphere with the nice music and window-shop seating, and has been a nice place to do work, watch a movie on my iPad, or have interesting conversations with people in the shared seating area. Now, above all of this is their impressive customer service!  Early on I was welcomed como familia (like family), and they have continued to make me feel like an appreciated customer in several ways.  The owner Juan, his father (also Juan), his mother Aracely, his cousin Cynthia, and one of their main employees Iselda have all been great, whether on the phone or in person, remembering my usual order, asking how I‚Äôm doing, or handing me my order with a smile üòÉüëç.  Stop by this wonderful family run business; enjoy the tasty food and drinks, the hospitable family feel, and experience part of their heritage!  You‚Äôll be glad that you did üòé<//review>

<rating>5< /rating>< review>
Wow, this was my first time going to this restaurant and there is something very authentic about the food. I ordered the bbq burrito and I have to tell you the meat was surprisingly good (I could have appreciated more of it) the rice could have used a little more flavor, the beans remind me of when I was younger (do you remember what beans used to taste like?)
The one exception that I have to point out above everything else... the condiments! (even fried onions) the jalapenos although cut were still crisp and crunchy, the sauces were awesome, especially the spicy oil sauce (although it numbed my room mates mouth for awhile) I found the taste and heat absolutely wonderful! its rare that I want to go back to get a bucket of sauce (or even eat all the sauce from most places) I think I need to find a bucket! ;)
Thank You, keep up the great work and I will be back!</review>

<date>1521178728126<//date><Review>Order here if you:
- like uncooked pizza dough
- want to get a rude service (plus getting yelled at)
- want to be treated like you are a cheapskate asking for a free pizza when you were just telling them that their pizza is undercooked.

I really wanted to like this place because it is very close to my apartment. However, they got the worst customer service. I have ordered few times here and never had any problem before until today. The pizza I received was not fully cooked. The dough was still sticky in the middle and so soft that I could mold it and bake a pie. The dough literally looked like melted mozzarella cheese. (See the pictures)

I called the store, and they treated me like I was trying to get a free pizza. I can understand that because I worked in a restaurant before, and saw few people doing that. I wanted to be nice to them and just tell them they need to watch out for undercooked food. Then, I would probably have throw the pizza into my oven and just cook it myself. However, the way they instantly talked rudely at me just turned me off. Let me tell you if the Pizzaman workers are reading this: I DON'T NEED A FREE PIZZA BECAUSE I CAN AFFORD ONE MYSELF. ALL I WANTED WAS A FULLY-COOKED PIZZA! They talked so rudely and they were pissed at me for telling them that the pizza is under-cooked. They told me (almost yelled) that I should have asked for a "well-done pizza." I have never ordered a well-done pizza from anywhere else and never received a undercooked pizza, so I just assumed that this place cooks their dough all the way. Also, when I ordered with them before, the pizzas were fully-cooked. However, they are telling me that it is my fault that the pizza is undercooked.

They asked rudely if I want to get another pizza, and I didn't want to because who knows if they are going to contaminate my food. I didn't want to risk getting a contaminated pizza because they sounded angry and rude. I don't trust people who get easily tilted to handle my food.

***They gave me a refund on the pizza, but they said, "I can't refund it if there's more than two slices gone." For sure, they thought I was trying to get free food because I told them my husband and I didn't finish our two slices because of the dough. smh. The delivery guy came to pick up the pizza, and he even opened the box to see if we didn't eat more than two slices. Also, they never apologized for anything.***

To be honest, their food isn't that good, so I am fine with not ordering here. Their wings are tooooooo greasy and blend. The pizza is "eh." I just ordered here before because it just opened and tried to find a good pizza place.

See the pictures:
The dough looks like cheese and so sticky that it sticks to the box like glue. I can also mold the uncooked dough! The crust looks cooked, but in the middle it is still sticky. You can see that the color in the middle is darker and looks wet, because IT IS.

I will never order from this place again, and stop my family/friends/neighbors from ordering here.<//Review>< username>

< rating>
5</rating>
< review>
Not getting the bad reviews posted here. Pizza Man is the BEST Neopolitan-style pizza in Pasadena. Period. We've been ordering from them for 5 years, since before they were on GrubHub or any other delivery service. We spent a month in Italy and Pizza Man is the closest you will get to real Italian pizza, without a doubt. And they will take orders until 11pm, which, for Pasadena, is quite accommodating.

However, be aware. If you are ordering via a service (Grubhub, Doordash, etc), I don't think they get the "special instructions." In other words, if you want parmesan cheese, red pepper flakes, plasticware, etc, you actually must call the restaurant after you order online and let them know. This is no condemnation on the pizza itself, but rather on the delivery companies.

When we're craving pizza, the only place we order from is Pizza Man. Fast, hot, delicious. Try the thin crust. It's insanely good.< /review>

I came in with an excruciating toothache and needed it extracted. I came in as a walk in and I understand that there were patients before me so I did have to wait a while. <Text>I hadn't been to see a dentist in 17 years.   I dont have a particular reason- just never had any pain.  But with that said, All people that are afraid of the dentist should have gone with me today.  I had 2 appointments today.  From the moment I walked in I was helped by some very beautiful young ladies and seated. I was called to meet the ortho and a young- also beautiful woman began to prep me and answered any and all questions I had.   I met the ortho surgeon who was male and also very nice. ( My teeth are drifting apart and I was concerned I would have rotten teeth, unusable for braces  It had been 17 years afterall.)  I was given a good examination by somebody with knowledge. I was deemed good for braces.  I have no money so it's for the future.
My 2nd appt was for a cleaning- I really feared bad news from the dentist.  I was called 10 min after my prior appt. I had x rays done and had to bite on plastic which wasn't so bad I just have a small gag reflex with the plastic throwaway sleeve they cover the biting part with.  The gorgeous young lady that took the xrays was also extremely helpful in any of the Q&A I had.  I was moved to a different room where they would actually do the cleaning.  I met the dentist-  This guy was middle aged and cracking jokes.  He is awesome.  I feared his news after a young woman(also beautiful) came and took different pictures of my teeth and.. dried them.  The dentist saw me and had me open wide, he searched for cavities and other complications and found none- which is awesome! Yay Me!  After sooo long of not seeing a dentist I really didnt expect that.  I try to take care of my teeth but I dont floss.  It was now time for my cleaning.  I think I am like everyone when I say having power tools in your mouth can be quite scary.  But, BUT- they've made leaps and bounds in dentistry since 17 years ago.  The tools are very small and not very noisy.  I braced for some sort of pain while they turned on the tool and started cleaning- there was none.  The most awkward anything was the sensation of the tool doing its job in front and behind my teeth.  My dentist finished cleaning , cracked some more jokes and ran off to some other beautiful smile to help.  A young woman chatted with me while finishing with flouride and asked me to rate them and so I am here!  These guys kick ass, All of em! Everyone that I spoke to or had questions with was genuinely professional,  pleasant, and courteous. ... and beautiful.

I understand that wait times could be different and that you may need more than just a cleaning.  In my experience when you find a good place filled with heartfelt, wonderful people,- it normally stays that way.  This Western Dental has it in spades and I recommend any and all to go and check em out.

Sorry to all at Western Dental in Banning I am extremely horrible with names.  You guys keep kickin ass, I'll see you guys soon :)< /Text>< Rate>
